    <th colspan="2">
      <a name="Service-001"></a> Term Name: Service</th>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>URI:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Service">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Service</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Namespace:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Label:
    </td>
    <td>Service</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Definition:
    </td>
    <td>A service is a system that provides one or more 
      functions of value to the end-user. Examples include: 
      a photocopying service, a banking service, an 
      authentication service, interlibrary loans, a Z39.50 
      or Web server.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>

    <th colspan="2">
      <a name="Software-001"></a> Term Name: Software</th>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>URI:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Software">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Software</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Namespace:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Label:
    </td>
    <td>Software</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Definition:
    </td>
    <td>Software is a computer program in source or 
      compiled form which may be available for installation 
      non-transiently on another machine. For software which 
      exists only to create an interactive environment, use 
      interactive instead.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Type of Term:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://dublincore.org/usage/documents/principles/#vocabulary-term">vocabulary-term</a>

    <th colspan="2">
      <a name="Sound-001"></a> Term Name: Sound</th>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>URI:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Sound">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Sound</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Namespace:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Label:
    </td>
    <td>Sound</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Definition:
    </td>
    <td>A sound is a resource whose content is primarily 
      intended to be rendered as audio. For example - a 
      music playback file format, an audio compact disc, 
      and recorded speech or sounds.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Type of Term:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://dublincore.org/usage/documents/principles/#vocabulary-term">vocabulary-term</a>

    <th colspan="2">
      <a name="StillImage-003"></a> Term Name: StillImage</th>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>URI:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/StillImage">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/StillImage</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Namespace:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Name for Table:
    </td>
    <td>dcmitype-StillImage</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Label:
    </td>
    <td>Still Image</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Definition:
    </td>
    <td>A static visual representation.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Comment:
    </td>
    <td>Examples include paintings, drawings, graphic designs, plans and maps. Recommended best practice is to assign the type Text to images of textual materials. Instances of the type Still Image must also be describable as instances of the broader type Image.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Type of Term:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#Class">Class</a>

    <th colspan="2">
      <a name="StillImage-001"></a> Term Name: StillImage</th>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>URI:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/StillImage">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/StillImage</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Namespace:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Label:
    </td>
    <td>Still Image</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Definition:
    </td>
    <td>A static visual representation. Examples of
      still images are: paintings, drawings, graphic designs,
      plans and maps.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Comment:
    </td>
    <td>Recommended best practice is to assign the type
      "text" to images of textual materials. Instances of
      the type "Still Image" must also be describable as
      instances of the broader type "Image".</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>

    <th colspan="2">
      <a name="Text-003"></a> Term Name: Text</th>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>URI:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Text">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/Text</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Namespace:
    </td>
    <td>
      <a href="http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/">http://purl.org/dc/dcmitype/</a>
    </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Name for Table:
    </td>
    <td>dcmitype-Text</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Label:
    </td>
    <td>Text</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Definition:
    </td>
    <td>A resource consisting primarily of words for reading.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Comment:
    </td>
    <td>Examples include books, letters, dissertations, poems, newspapers, articles, archives of mailing lists. Note that facsimiles or images of texts are still of the genre Text.</td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td>Type of Term:
    </td>

      <a href="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#Class">Class</a>
